   <h1 class="firstHeading" id="firstHeading" lang="en">
    List of 20th-century lunar eclipses
   </h1>
   <div class="mw-body-content" id="bodyContent">
    <div class="noprint" id="siteSub">
     From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia
    </div>
    <div id="contentSub">
    </div>
    <div class="mw-jump" id="jump-to-nav">
     Jump to:
     <a href="#mw-head">
      navigation
     </a>
     ,
     <a href="#p-search">
      search
     </a>
    </div>
    <div class="mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr" id="mw-content-text" lang="en">
     <div class="mw-parser-output">
      <p>
       A total of 230
       <a href="/wiki/Lunar_eclipse" title="Lunar eclipse">
        lunar eclipses
       </a>
       took place in the 20th century: 83 penumbral, 66 partial and 81 total.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-1">
         [1]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       See also:
       <a href="/wiki/Lists_of_lunar_eclipses" title="Lists of lunar eclipses">
        Lists of lunar eclipses
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/List_of_19th-century_lunar_eclipses" title="List of 19th-century lunar eclipses">
        List of 19th-century lunar eclipses
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/List_of_21st-century_lunar_eclipses" title="List of 21st-century lunar eclipses">
        List of 21st-century lunar eclipses
       </a>
      </p>
      <h2>
       <span id="List_of_lunar_eclipses_between_1901_and_2000.5B2.5D">
       </span>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="List_of_lunar_eclipses_between_1901_and_2000[2]">
        List of lunar eclipses between 1901 and 2000
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-2">
         <a href="#cite_note-2">
          [2]
         </a>
        </sup>
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_20th-century_lunar_eclipses&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: List of lunar eclipses between 1901 and 2000[2]">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <p>
       Eclipses from 2001 to 2002 are included on the end to complete the final set.
      </p>
